\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Are\_Points\_Sorted\_AntiClockWise()}{Are\_Points\_Sorted\_AntiClockWise()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_grid___computations_8cpp_a0bdffb27693c14d6cb4ef62eb5bd5d7f_a0bdffb27693c14d6cb4ef62eb5bd5d7f} 
bool Are\+\_\+\+Points\+\_\+\+Sorted\+\_\+\+Anti\+Clock\+Wise (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{definitions_8h_ae73d8ca7e27dfe59448bcfcbe537f514_ae73d8ca7e27dfe59448bcfcbe537f514}{V\+\_\+D}} $>$ \&}]{grouped\+Points}{, }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{definitions_8h_ae73d8ca7e27dfe59448bcfcbe537f514_ae73d8ca7e27dfe59448bcfcbe537f514}{V\+\_\+D}} \&}]{Centroid}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Sorts a set of points in anti-\/clockwise order around their centroid. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em Points} & A flat vector of coordinates representing 3D points. The vector should have a size that is a multiple of 3, where each triplet (x, y, z) represents a point.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Assumptions\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The input vector {\ttfamily Points} is structured as a flat array of 3D points.
\item The function computes the centroid of the points and sorts them based on their angle relative to the centroid in the XY plane.
\item The Z-\/coordinate is ignored during sorting. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{Read\_Grid@{Read\_Grid}!Grid\_Computations.cpp@{Grid\_Computations.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Read\_Grid()}{Read\_Grid()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_grid___computations_8cpp_a663d4b3ae06e638c2f2e82ad437e831e_a663d4b3ae06e638c2f2e82ad437e831e} 
void Read\+\_\+\+Grid (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const string \&}]{ipfile}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Reads the input grid file and constructs physical cells, evaluates face areas, normals, and cell volumes. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ipfile} & The path to the input grid file.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Function for reading input grid file. This file has particular format written by me for reading the grid data. The grid file contains the information of the vertices of the cell followed by the cell and its neighbours information in .txt file. It takes a file containing data of grid and constructs Physical Cells, evaluates its face areas, normals and cell volumes. Creates the storage vectors for the above said variables.
